CodeSystem: Procedimentos da Tabela SUS

Summary

Defining URL:http://www.saude.gov.br/fhir/r4/CodeSystem/BRTabelaSUS
Version:0.1.0
Name:Tabela de Procedimentos, medicamentos e OPM do SUS
Title:Procedimentos da Tabela SUS
Status:Active as of 2020-04-07T18:22:41.0609621+00:00
Definition:

Padroniza os códigos e as nomenclaturas dos procedimentos, medicamentos e OPM para as informações trafegadas no SUS.

Publisher:Rede Nacional de Dados em Saúde
Content:Complete: All the concepts defined by the code system are included in the code system resource
Source Resource:XML / JSON / Turtle

This Code system is referenced in the content logical definition of the following value sets:

  • BRProcedimentosNacionais
  • BRTipoObservacao

This code system http://www.saude.gov.br/fhir/r4/CodeSystem/BRTabelaSUS defines the following codes:
